<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kléitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеиться.html>кле́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kléitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to glue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клеиться.html>кле́ится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bumága <b>kléitsja</b> lexkó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">paper <b>glues</b> easily</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go well <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клеиться.html>кле́ился</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razgovór ne <b>kléilsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the conversation did not <b>go well</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клеиться.html>кле́ится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>kléitsja</b> u nas s tobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we're not <b>getting along</b> with you</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seduce, to lure</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>клей</a> (6313)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">klej</i>. From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klajjaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gley-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to glue, stick together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>клей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>кле́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>кле́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>кле́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glue</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клейкий.html>кле́йкий</a> (19057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клейкий.html>кле́йкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kléjkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)кле́йче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sticky, tenacious (clinging to an object or surface; adhesive)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:клейкий.html>кле́йкая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kléjkaja</b> lénta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">duct tape</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***клеймо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клеймо́</a> (13981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Dialectally also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">клейно́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klejnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клеймо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klejmó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">клейно́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klejnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">кляймо́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kljajmó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">кляйно́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kljajnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Per Vasmer, borrowed from unattested <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*kleim</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glue, clay, mortar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klaimaz</i>. (Only <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kleimen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smear, to oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is attested, but the vowel sequence <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ей-</span> is most easily derived from Old High German or Old Norse among the Germanic languages, and Vasmer specifically denies a derivation from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kleima</i>.) Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">clām</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clay, mud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cloam</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">klēm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glue, mortar, plaster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клеймо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klejmó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клейма́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>кле́йма</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>кле́йм</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brand, stamp, identification mark</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stain, taint as in tainted reputation</li></ol>

***клетка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тка</a> (1806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">клѣтъка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klětŭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klětъka</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klětь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klětъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cage, coop, cell</li>
<li>square, check <i>(checkered pattern)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v klétku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quad ruled; quadrille ruled</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bumága v <b>klétku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">quadrille ruled paper; quad ruled paper; graph paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тетрадь.html>тетра́дь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tetrádʹ v <b>klétku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">quadrille ruled notebook; quad ruled notebook</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:клеточный.html>кле́точное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строение.html>строе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>klétočnoje</b> strojénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cellular texture</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klìkati</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликать.html>кли́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klíkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликнуть.html>кли́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликать.html>кли́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klíkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кликнуть.html>кли́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klìknǫti</i>.
